And he would raise his voice saying "we refuse" and prolong it. This has also been narrated with a metrical alteration in the authentic collection as well. Likewise it is established that he said on the day of Hunayn, while riding the mule, advancing it into the throats of the enemy:

"I am the Prophet, no lie, I am the son of Abd al-Muttalib."

But they said: this occurred coincidentally, without any intent to compose verse by meter; rather it came upon the tongue without any intention toward it.

Likewise what is established in the two Sahihs from Jundab ibn Abdullah, who said: We were with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ in a cave, and his finger was struck, so he said:

"Are you anything but a finger that has bled, and in the path of Allah what you have encountered?"

And there will come, at His statement {except for al-lamam} [al-Najm: 32], the recitation of:

"If You forgive, O Allah, You forgive abundantly, and which servant of Yours has not sinned?"

None of this contradicts the fact that he ﷺ was not taught poetry, nor was it befitting for him. For Allah the Almighty only taught him the mighty Qur'an, that {falsehood does not come to it from before it or from behind it, a revelation from One Who is Wise and Praiseworthy} [Fussilat: 42]. It is not poetry, as a faction among the ignorant disbelievers of Quraysh claimed, nor is it soothsaying, nor fabrication, nor sorcery handed down, despite the various sayings of the misguided and the opinions of the ignorant regarding it. His natural disposition ﷺ rejected the craft of poetry, both by innate nature and by the sacred law, as Abu Dawud narrated, saying:

[chain] Abdullah ibn Amr said: [I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say]: "I do not care what may befall me, whether I drink a theriac, or wear an amulet, or compose poetry of my own accord." Abu Dawud alone narrated it.

Imam Ahmad, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Abu Nawfal said: I asked A'ishah: Did the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to have poetry recited in his presence and listen to it? She said: It was the most hateful of speech to him.

It was reported from Aisha: "The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was pleased by comprehensive supplications, and he left aside what fell between that."

Abu Dawud said: [chain] Abu al-Walid al-Tayalisi told us, Shu'bah told us, from al-A'mash, from Abu Salih, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ: "That the inside of one of you should fill with pus is better for him than that it should fill with poetry." He was alone in transmitting it by this route, and its chain meets the standard of the two Shaykhs (Bukhari and Muslim), though they did not include it in their collections.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Bd told us, Qaza'ah ibn Suwayd al-Bahili told us, from Asim ibn Makhlad, from Abu al-Ash'ath al-San'ani (ح), and al-Ashyab also told us, saying: from Ibn Asim, from [Abu] al-Ash'ath, from Shaddad ibn Aws, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever composes a line of poetry after the last night prayer, his prayer for that night will not be accepted." This is a gharib (singular) hadith by this route, and none of the authors of the six canonical collections included it. What is meant by this is the composing of poetry, not merely reciting it, and Allah knows best. Moreover, there is poetry which is permissible, such as the satirizing of the polytheists which the poets of Islam engaged in, like Hassan ibn Thabit, Ka'b ibn Malik, Abdullah ibn Rawahah, and others like them, may Allah be pleased with them all. There is also poetry containing wisdom, admonitions, and matters of proper conduct, as is found in the poetry of a group from the Jahiliyyah (pre-Islamic era), among them Umayyah ibn Abi al-Salt, about whom the Prophet ﷺ said: "His poetry believed but his heart disbelieved." Some of the Companions recited a hundred lines of his poetry to the Prophet ﷺ, and after each line the Prophet would say "Go on," meaning he wanted to hear more, so the Companion would recite more of it to him.

Abu Dawud narrated, from the hadith of Ubayy ibn Ka'b, Buraydah ibn al-Husayb, and Abdullah ibn Abbas, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed some eloquent speech is like magic, and indeed some poetry contains wisdom."

For this reason, Allah, exalted is He, said: {And We did not teach him poetry}, meaning Muhammad ﷺ; Allah did not teach him poetry. {Nor is it fitting for him}, that is, it would not be proper or suitable for him. {It is not except a reminder and a clear Qur'an}, meaning: this thing which We taught him is nothing but {a reminder and a clear Qur'an}, that is, clear, plain, and evident to whoever reflects upon it and ponders it deeply. For this reason He said: {That it may warn whoever is alive}, meaning: that this clear Qur'an may warn every living being upon the face of the earth, just as He said: {That I may warn you thereby, and whomever it reaches} [al-An'am: 19], and He said: {And whoever disbelieves in it from among the factions, the Fire is his promised place} [Hud: 17]. Only one whose heart is alive and whose insight is illuminated benefits from its warning, just as Qatadah said: "Alive of heart, alive of sight." Al-Dahhak said: it means one who is rational and sound of mind. {And that the word may be justly carried out against the disbelievers}, meaning: it is a mercy for the believer and a proof against the disbeliever.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ ابْنِ آدَمَ أَنَّهُ كُلَّمَا طَالَ عُمْرُهُ رُدَّ إِلَى الضَّعْفِ بَعْدَ الْقُوَّةِ وَالْعَجْزِ بَعْدَ النَّشَاطِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ ضَعْفٍ ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ ضَعْفٍ قُوَّةً ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ قُوَّةٍ ضَعْفًا وَشَيْبَةً يَخْلُقُ مَا يَشَاءُ وَهُوَ الْعَلِيمُ الْقَدِيرُ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٥٤] . وَقَالَ: ﴿وَمِنْكُمْ مَنْ يُرَدُّ إِلَى أَرْذَلِ الْعُمُرِ لِكَيْلا يَعْلَمَ مِنْ بَعْدِ عِلْمٍ شَيْئًا﴾ [الْحَجِّ: ٥] .

وَالْمُرَادُ مِنْ هَذَا -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ-الإخبارُ عَنْ هَذِهِ الدَّارِ بِأَنَّهَا دَارُ زَوَالٍ وَانْتِقَالٍ، لَا دَارُ دَوَامٍ وَاسْتِقْرَارٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَفَلا يَعْقِلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَتَفَكَّرُونَ بِعُقُولِهِمْ فِي ابْتِدَاءِ خَلْقِهِمْ ثُمَّ صَيْرُورَتِهِمْ إِلَى [نَفْسِ] الشَّبيبَة، ثُمَّ إِلَى الشَّيْخُوخَةِ؛ لِيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّهُمْ خُلقوا لِدَارٍ أُخْرَى، لَا زَوَالَ لَهَا وَلَا انْتِقَالَ مِنْهَا، وَلَا مَحِيدَ عَنْهَا، وَهِيَ الدَّارُ الْآخِرَةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا عَلَّمْنَاهُ الشِّعْرَ وَمَا يَنْبَغِي لَهُ﴾ : يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ نَبِيِّهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ : أَنَّهُ مَا عَلَّمَهُ الشِّعْرَ، ﴿وَمَا يَنْبَغِي لَهُ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا هُوَ فِي طَبْعِهِ، فَلَا يُحْسِنُهُ وَلَا يُحِبُّهُ، وَلَا تَقْتَضِيهِ جِبِلَّته؛ وَلِهَذَا وَرَدَ أَنَّهُ، عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ، كَانَ لَا يَحْفَظُ بَيْتًا عَلَى وزنٍ مُنْتَظِمٍ، بَلْ إِنْ أَنْشَدَهُ زَحَّفه أَوْ لَمْ يُتِمَّهُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو زُرْعة الرَّازِّيُّ: حُدِّثت عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ مُجَالِدٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: مَا وَلَد عَبْدُ الْمُطَّلِبِ ذَكَرًا وَلَا أُنْثَى إِلَّا يَقُولُ الشِّعر، إِلَّا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ. ذَكَرَهُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ "عُتْبَةَ بْنِ أَبِي لَهَبٍ" الَّذِي أَكَلَهُ السَّبُع بِالزَّرْقَاءِ. 

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَلَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ -هُوَ الْبَصْرِيُّ-قَالَ: إِنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَتَمَثَّلُ بِهَذَا الْبَيْتِ:

كَفَى بالإسْلام والشيْب للمرْء نَاهيًا

فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ:

كَفى الشَّيْبُ وَالْإِسْلَامُ لِلْمَرْءِ نَاهِيًا ...

قَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ، أَوْ عُمَرُ: أَشْهَدُ أَنَّكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ، يَقُولُ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَمَا عَلَّمْنَاهُ الشِّعْرَ وَمَا يَنْبَغِي لَهُ﴾ .

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى الْبَيْهَقِيُّ فِي الدَّلَائِلِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: لِلْعَبَّاسِ بْنِ مِرْدَاسٍ السُّلَمِيِّ: "أَنْتَ الْقَائِلُ:

أَتَجْعَلَ نَهبي ونَهْب العُبَيد بَيْنَ الْأَقْرَعِ وَعُيَيْنَةَ".

فَقَالَ: إِنَّمَا هُوَ: "بَيْنَ عُيَيْنَةَ والأقرع" فقال: "الكل سواء". يَعْنِي: فِي الْمَعْنَى، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ.

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ السُّهَيْلِيُّ فِي "الرَّوْضِ الْأُنُفِ" لِهَذَا التَّقْدِيمِ وَالتَّأْخِيرِ الَّذِي وَقَعَ فِي كَلَامِهِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي هَذَا الْبَيْتِ مُنَاسِبَةً أَغْرَبَ فِيهَا، حَاصِلُهَا شَرَفُ الْأَقْرَعِ بْنِ حَابِسٍ عَلَى عُيَيْنَة بْنِ بَدْرٍ الْفَزَارِيِّ؛ لِأَنَّهُ ارْتَدَّ أَيَّامَ الصِّدِّيقِ، بِخِلَافِ ذَاكَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى الْأُمَوِيُّ فِي مَغَازِيهِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ جَعَلَ يَمْشِي بَيْنَ الْقَتْلَى يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: "نُفلق هَامًا..................................".

فَيَقُولُ الصِّدِّيقُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، مُتَمِّمًا لِلْبَيْتِ:

..... مِنْ رجَال أعزَّةٍ ... عَلَيْنَا وَهُم كَانُوا أعَقَّ وَأظلما ...

وَهَذَا لِبَعْضِ شُعَرَاءِ الْعَرَبِ فِي قَصِيدَةٍ لَهُ، وَهِيَ فِي الْحَمَاسَةِ. 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا هُشَيْم، حَدَّثَنَا مُغِيرَةُ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا اسْتَرَاثَ الْخَبَرَ، تَمَثَّلَ فِيهِ بِبَيْتِ طَرَفَة:

ويَأْتِيكَ بالأخْبار مَنْ لَمْ تُزَوِّدِ

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي "الْيَوْمِ وَاللَّيْلَةِ" مِنْ طَرِيقِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ مُهَاجِرٍ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْهَا. وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ أَيْضًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْمِقْدَامِ بْنِ شُرَيْح بْنِ هَانِئٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، كَذَلِكَ. ثُمَّ قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ. هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ. 

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا يُوسُفُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا أُسَامَةُ، عَنْ زَائِدَةَ، عَنْ سِمَاك، عَنْ عِكْرِمَة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَتَمَثَّلُ مِنَ الْأَشْعَارِ:

وَيَأتيكَ بالأخْبَار مَنْ لَمْ تُزَوِّدِ ...

ثُمَّ قَالَ: رَوَاهُ غَيْرُ زَائِدَةَ، عَنْ سِمَاك، عَنْ عِكرمة، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ. 

وَهَذَا فِي شِعْرِ طَرَفَةَ بْنِ الْعَبْدِ، فِي مُعَلَّقَتِهِ الْمَشْهُورَةِ، وَهَذَا الْمَذْكُورُ [هُوَ عَجُزُ بَيْتٍ] مِنْهَا، أَوَّلُهُ:

سَتُبْدي لكَ الأيامُ مَا كُنْتَ جَاهلا ... وَيَأتيك بالأخْبَارِ مَنْ لَمْ تُزَوِّدِ ...

وَيَأتيكَ بالأخْبَار مَنْ لَمْ تَبِع لهُ ... بَتَاتا وَلَمْ تَضرب لَهُ وَقْتَ مَوْعِدِ 

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ: أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ الْحَافِظُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو حَفْصٍ عُمَرُ بن أحمد بن نُعَيْمٍ -وَكِيلُ الْمُتَّقِي بِبَغْدَادَ-حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُحَمَّدٍ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ هِلَالٍ النَّحْوِيُّ الضَّرِيرُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَمْرٍو الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: مَا جَمَعَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْتَ شِعْرٍ قَطُّ، إِلَّا بَيْتًا وَاحِدًا. 

تَفَاءلْ بِمَا تَهْوَى يَكُنْ فَلَقَلَّمَا ... يُقَالُ لِشَيْءٍ كَانَ إِلَّا تَحَقَّقَا 

سَأَلْتُ شَيْخَنَا الْحَافِظَ أَبَا الْحَجَّاجِ الْمِزِّيَّ عَنْ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ، فَقَالَ: هُوَ مُنْكَرٌ. وَلَمْ يُعْرَفْ شَيْخُ الْحَاكِمِ، وَلَا الضَّرِيرُ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَرُوبة عَنْ قَتَادَةَ: قِيلَ لِعَائِشَةَ: هَلْ كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَتَمَثَّلُ بِشَيْءٍ مِنَ الشِّعْرِ؟ قَالَتْ: كَانَ أبغضَ الْحَدِيثَ إِلَيْهِ، غَيْرَ أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَتَمَثَّلُ بِبَيْتِ أَخِي بَنِي قَيْسٍ، فَيَجْعَلُ أَوَّلَهُ آخِرَهُ، وَآخِرَهُ أَوَّلَهُ. فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ لَيْسَ هَكَذَا. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إني وَاللَّهِ مَا أَنَا بِشَاعِرٍ وَلَا يَنْبَغِي لِي". رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَهَذَا لَفْظُهُ. 

وَقَالَ مَعْمَرٌ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ عَائِشَةَ سُئلت: هَلْ كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَتَمَثَّلُ بِشَيْءٍ مِنَ الشِّعْرِ؟ فَقَالَتْ: لَا إِلَّا بَيْتَ طَرَفَة:

سَتُبْدي لكَ الأيامُ مَا كُنْتَ جَاهلا ... وَيَأْتيك بالأخبارِ مَنْ لَمْ تُزَوِّدِ ...

فَجَعَلَ يَقُولُ: "مَن لَمْ تُزَوّد بِالْأَخْبَارِ". فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: لَيْسَ هَذَا هَكَذَا. فَقَالَ: "إِنِّي لَسْتُ بِشَاعِرٍ، وَلَا يَنْبَغِي لِي" 

وَثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَنَّهُ، عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ، تَمَثَّلَ يَوْمَ حَفْرِ الْخَنْدَقِ بِأَبْيَاتِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ رَوَاحَةَ، وَلَكِنْ تَبَعًا لِقَوْلِ أَصْحَابِهِ، فَإِنَّهُمْ يرتجزون وهم يحفرون، فيقولون:

لاهُمَّ لوْلا أنت مَا اهْتَدَيْنَا مَا اهْتَدَيْنَا ... وَلا تَصَدَّقْنَا وَلا صَلَّيْنَا ...

فَأَنزلَنْ سَكِينَةً عَلَيْنَا ... وَثَبِّت الأقْدَامَ إنْ لاقَيْنَا ...

إِنَّ الْأُلَى قَدْ بَغَوا عَليْنَا ... إذَا أرَادُوا فِتْنَةً أَبَيْنَا ...

وَيَرْفَعُ صَوْتَهُ بِقَوْلِهِ: "أَبَيْنَا" وَيَمُدُّهَا . وَقَدْ رُوِيَ هَذَا بِزِحَافٍ فِي الصَّحِيحِ أَيْضًا. وَكَذَلِكَ ثَبَتَ أَنَّهُ قَالَ يَوْمَ حُنَيْنٍ وَهُوَ رَاكِبٌ الْبَغْلَةَ، يُقدم بِهَا فِي نُحُورِ الْعَدُوِّ:

أَنَا النَّبِيّ لَا كَذِبْ ... أنَا ابْنُ عُبْد المُطَّلِبْ 

لَكِنْ قَالُوا: هَذَا وَقَعَ اتِّفَاقًا مِنْ غَيْرِ قَصْدٍ لِوَزْنِ شِعْرٍ، بَلْ جَرَى عَلَى اللِّسَانِ مِنْ غَيْرِ قَصْدٍ إِلَيْهِ.

وَكَذَلِكَ مَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ جُنْدَب بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهُ قَالَ: كُنَّا مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ في غار @ فَنَكِبت أُصْبُعُهُ، فَقَالَ:

هَلْ أنْت إِلَّا إصْبَعٌ دَمِيت ... وَفِي سَبيل اللَّهِ مَا لَقِيت 

وَسَيَأْتِي عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِلا اللَّمَمَ﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٣٢] إِنْشَادُ 

إنْ تَغْفر اللَّهُمَّ تَغْفِرْ جَمَّا ... وَأيُّ عَبْدٍ لكَ مَا ألَمَّا ...

وَكُلُّ هَذَا لَا يُنَافِي كَوْنَهُ ﷺ مَا عُلِّم شِعْرًا وَلَا يَنْبَغِي لَهُ؛ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى إِنَّمَا عَلَّمَهُ الْقُرْآنُ الْعَظِيمُ، الذِي ﴿لَا يَأْتِيهِ الْبَاطِلُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَلا مِنْ خَلْفِهِ تَنزيلٌ مِنْ حَكِيمٍ حَمِيدٍ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٤٢] . وَلَيْسَ هُوَ بِشِعْرٍ كَمَا زَعَمَهُ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْ جَهَلَةِ كُفَّارِ قُرَيْشٍ، وَلَا كِهَانَةٍ، وَلَا مُفْتَعِلٍ، وَلَا سِحْرٍ يُؤثر، كَمَا تَنَوَّعَتْ فِيهِ أَقْوَالُ الضُّلال وَآرَاءُ الجُهَّال. وَقَدْ كَانَتْ سَجِيَّتُهُ ﷺ تَأْبَى صِنَاعَةَ الشِّعْرِ طَبْعًا وَشَرْعًا، كَمَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ قَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُمَر، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ يَزِيدَ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدٌ بْنُ أَبِي أَيُّوبَ، حَدَّثَنَا شُرَحْبِيلُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ المَعَافري، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ رَافِعٍ التَّنُوخِيِّ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرٍو يَقُولُ : [سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ] : مَا أُبَالِي مَا أُوتِيْتُ إِنْ أَنَا شَربت تِرْيَاقًا، أَوْ تَعَلَّقْتُ تَمِيمَةً، أَوْ قُلْتُ الشِّعْرَ مِنْ قِبَلِ نَفْسِي". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَبُو دَاوُدَ. 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَهْدِيٍّ، عَنْ الْأُسُودِ بْنِ شَيْبَانَ، عَنْ أَبِي نَوْفَلٍ قَالَ: سألتُ عَائِشَةَ: أَكَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَتَسَامَعُ عِنْدَهُ الشِّعْرَ؟ فَقَالَتْ: كَانَ أَبْغَضَ الْحَدِيثِ إِلَيْهِ. وَقَالَ عَنْ عَائِشَةُ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُعْجِبُهُ الْجَوَامِعُ مِنَ الدُّعَاءِ، وَيَدَعُ مَا بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ. 

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْوَلِيدِ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: "لِأَنَّ يَمْتَلِئُ جَوْفُ أَحَدِكُمْ قَيْحًا، خَيْرٌ لَهُ مِنْ أَنْ يَمْتَلِئَ شِعْرًا". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، وَإِسْنَادُهُ عَلَى شَرْطِ الشَّيْخَيْنِ، وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ. 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا بُرَيْدٌ، حَدَّثَنَا قَزَعةُ بْنُ سُوَيْد الْبَاهِلِيُّ، عَنْ عَاصِمِ بْنِ مَخْلَد، عَنْ أَبِي الْأَشْعَثِ، الصَّنْعَانِيِّ (ح) وَحَدَّثَنَا الْأَشْيَبُ فَقَالَ: عَنِ ابْنِ عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ [أَبِي] الْأَشْعَثِ عَنْ شَدَّاد بْنِ أَوْسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ قَرَضِ بَيْتَ شِعْرٍ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ الْآخِرَةِ، لَمْ تُقْبَلْ لَهُ صلاة تلك الليلة". وَهَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجْهُ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ الْكُتُبِ السِّتَّةِ. وَالْمُرَادُ بِذَلِكَ نَظْمُهُ لَا إِنْشَادُهُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. عَلَى أَنَّ الشِّعْرَ فِيهِ مَا هُوَ مَشْرُوعٌ، وَهُوَ هِجَاءُ الْمُشْرِكِينَ الَّذِي كَانَ يَتَعَاطَاهُ شُعَرَاءُ الْإِسْلَامِ، كَحَسَّانَ بْنِ ثَابِتٍ، وَكَعْبِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، وَعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ رَوَاحة، وَأَمْثَالِهِمْ وَأَضْرَابِهِمْ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ. وَمِنْهُ مَا فِيهِ حِكَمٌ وَمَوَاعِظُ وَآدَابٌ، كَمَا يُوجَدُ فِي شِعْرِ جَمَاعَةٍ مِنَ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ، وَمِنْهُمْ أُمَيَّةُ بْنُ أَبِي الصَّلْتِ الَّذِي قال فيه النبي الله ﷺ: "آمَنَ شِعْرُهُ وَكَفَرَ قَلْبُهُ". وَقَدْ أَنْشَدَ بَعْضُ الصَّحَابَةِ مِنْهُ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ مِائَةَ بَيْتٍ، يَقُولُ عَقِبَ كُلِّ بَيْتٍ: "هِيهِ". يَعْنِي يَسْتَطْعِمُهُ، فَيَزِيدُهُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ. 

وَقَدْ رَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أُبي بْنِ كَعْبٍ، وبُريدة بْنِ الحُصَيْب ، وَعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ مِنَ الْبَيَانِ سِحْرًا، وَإِنَّ مِنَ الشِّعْرِ حِكَمًا" .

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا عَلَّمْنَاهُ الشِّعْرَ﴾ يَعْنِي: مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ مَا عَلَّمَهُ اللَّهُ شِعْرًا، ﴿وَمَا يَنْبَغِي لَهُ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا يَصْلُحُ لَهُ، ﴿إِنْ هُوَ إِلا ذِكْرٌ وَقُرْآنٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: مَا هَذَا الَّذِي عَلَّمْنَاهُ، ﴿إِلا ذِكْرٌ وَقُرْآنٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: بَيِّنٌ وَاضِحٌ جَلِيٌّ لِمَنْ تَأْمَّلَهُ وَتَدَبَّرَهُ. وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لِيُنْذِرَ مَنْ كَانَ حَيًّا﴾ أَيْ: لِيُنْذِرَ هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ الْبَيِّنُ كُلَّ حَيٍّ عَلَى وَجْهِ الْأَرْضِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿لأنْذِرَكُمْ بِهِ وَمَنْ بَلَغَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٩] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِهِ مِنَ الأحْزَابِ فَالنَّارُ مَوْعِدُهُ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٧] . وَإِنَّمَا يَنْتَفِعُ بِنِذَارَتِهِ مَنْ هُوَ حَيّ الْقَلْبِ، مُسْتَنِيرُ الْبَصِيرَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: حَيُّ الْقَلْبِ، حَيُّ الْبَصَرِ. وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: يَعْنِي: عَاقِلًا ﴿وَيَحِقَّ الْقَوْلُ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ رَحْمَةٌ لِلْمُؤْمِنِ، وَحُجَّةٌ عَلَى الكافر.

---

## 36:71-73 — verses 71-73 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted mentions the favor He bestowed upon His creatures through these livestock which He subjected for them, {so that they are their owners}. Qatadah said: meaning they are able to master them, that is, He made them overpower these animals while the animals remain submissive to them, unable to resist them. Rather, if a small child came to a camel, he would make it kneel down, and if he wished, he could make it stand and drive it, while the camel remains submissive and obedient to him. Likewise, even if the caravan consisted of a hundred camels or more, all of them would move at the pace set by a small child.

His statement: {and some of them they ride, and some of them they eat} means: some of them are what they ride upon in their journeys, and upon which they carry heavy loads to all directions and regions. {and some of them they eat}: when they wish, they slaughter them and cut them up for food.

{And for them in them are benefits} meaning: from their wool, their fur, and their hair, they make furnishings and goods for a time. {and drinks} meaning: from their milk, and their urine for those who seek medical treatment, and the like of that. {Will they not then be grateful?} meaning: will they not then affirm the oneness of the Creator of all this and the One who subjected it for them, and not associate any other with Him?

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى مَا أَنْعَمَ بِهِ عَلَى خَلْقِهِ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأَنْعَامِ الَّتِي سَخَّرَهَا لَهُمْ، ﴿فَهُمْ لَهَا مَالِكُونَ﴾ : قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: مُطِيقُونَ أَيْ: جَعَلَهُمْ يَقْهَرُونَهَا وَهِيَ ذَلِيلَةٌ لَهُمْ، لَا تَمْتَنِعُ مِنْهُمْ، بَلْ لَوْ جَاءَ صَغِيرٌ إِلَى بَعِيرٍ لَأَنَاخَهُ، وَلَوْ شَاءَ لَأَقَامَهُ وَسَاقَهُ، وَذَاكَ ذَلِيلٌ مُنْقَادٌ مَعَهُ. وَكَذَا لَوْ كَانَ القطَارُ مِائَةُ بَعِيرٍ أَوْ أَكْثَرُ، لَسَارَ الْجَمِيعُ بسيرِ صغيرٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَمِنْهَا رَكُوبُهُمْ وَمِنْهَا يَأْكُلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْهَا مَا يَرْكَبُونَ فِي الْأَسْفَارِ، وَيَحْمِلُونَ عَلَيْهِ الْأَثْقَالَ، إِلَى سَائِرِ الْجِهَاتِ وَالْأَقْطَارِ. ﴿وَمِنْهَا يَأْكُلُونَ﴾ إذا شاؤوا نَحَرُوا وَاجْتَزَرُوا.

﴿وَلَهُمْ فِيهَا مَنَافِعُ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أَصْوَافِهَا وَأَوْبَارِهَا وَأَشْعَارِهَا أَثَاثًا وَمَتَاعًا إِلَى حِينٍ، ﴿وَمَشَارِبُ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أَلْبَانِهَا وَأَبْوَالِهَا لِمَنْ يَتَدَاوَى، وَنَحْوِ ذَلِكَ. ﴿أَفَلا يَشْكُرُونَ﴾ ؟ أَيْ: أَفَلَا يُوَحِّدُون خَالِقَ ذَلِكَ وَمُسَخِّرَهُ، وَلَا يُشْرِكُونَ بِهِ غَيْرَهُ؟

---

## 36:74-76 — verses 74-76 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, denouncing the polytheists for taking rivals as gods alongside Allah, seeking thereby that these gods would help them, provide for them, and bring them near to Allah in close proximity.

Allah the Almighty says: {They are not able to help them}, meaning: the gods have no power to help their worshippers. Rather they are weaker than that, more lowly, more despicable, more contemptible, and more hidden away. Indeed they cannot even help themselves, nor take revenge upon whoever intends them harm, because they are inanimate matter that neither hears nor comprehends.

Regarding His saying: {while they are a host brought forth for them}, Mujahid said: meaning, at the reckoning. He means that these idols will be gathered and assembled on the Day of Resurrection, brought forth at the reckoning of their worshippers, so that this would be more thoroughly disgraceful for them and more conclusive as an establishment of proof against them.

Qatadah said: {They are not able to help them}, meaning the gods, {while they are a host brought forth for them}. The polytheists become angry on behalf of the gods in this world, while the gods bring them no good and repel no harm from them; they are nothing but idols.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said the same. This view is good, and it is the one chosen by Ibn Jarir, may Allah have mercy on him.

Regarding His saying: {So let not their saying grieve you}, meaning: their denial of you and their disbelief in Allah, {Indeed, We know what they conceal and what they proclaim}, meaning: We know all that they are engaged in, and We shall recompense them for their description and deal with them accordingly, on a Day when they will not find missing from their deeds anything great or small, neither trivial nor significant. Rather, all that they used to do, both of old and recent, will be presented before them.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُنْكِرًا عَلَى الْمُشْرِكِينَ فِي اتِّخَاذِهِمُ الْأَنْدَادَ آلِهَةً مَعَ اللَّهِ، يَبْتَغُونَ بِذَلِكَ أَنْ تَنْصُرَهُمْ تِلْكَ الْآلِهَةُ وَتَرْزُقَهُمْ وَتُقَرِّبَهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ زُلْفَى.

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ نَصْرَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَا تَقْدِرُ الْآلِهَةُ عَلَى نَصْرِ عَابِدِيهَا، بَلْ هِيَ أَضْعَفُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ وَأَقَلُّ وَأَذَلُّ وَأَحْقَرُ وَأَدْخَرُ، بَلْ لَا تَقْدِرُ عَلَى الِانْتِصَارِ لِأَنْفُسِهَا، وَلَا الِانْتِقَامِ مِمَّنْ أَرَادَهَا بِسُوءٍ؛ لِأَنَّهَا جَمَادٌ لَا تَسْمَعُ وَلَا تَعْقِلُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُمْ لَهُمْ جُنْدٌ مُحْضَرُونَ﴾ : قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي: عِنْدَ الْحِسَابِ، يُرِيدُ أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْأَصْنَامَ مَحْشُورَةٌ مَجْمُوعَةٌ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، مُحْضَرَةٌ عِنْدَ حِسَابِ عَابِدِيهَا؛ لِيَكُونَ ذَلِكَ أَبْلَغَ فِي خِزْيهم، وَأَدُلَّ عَلَيْهِمْ فِي إِقَامَةِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِمْ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ نَصْرَهُمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْآلِهَةَ، ﴿وَهُمْ لَهُمْ جُنْدٌ مُحْضَرُونَ﴾ ، وَالْمُشْرِكُونَ يَغْضَبُونَ لِلْآلِهَةِ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَهِيَ لَا تَسُوقُ إِلَيْهِمْ خَيْرًا، وَلَا تَدْفَعُ عَنْهُمْ سُوءًا، إِنَّمَا هِيَ أَصْنَامٌ.

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ. وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ حَسَنٌ، وَهُوَ اخْتِيَارُ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَلا يَحْزُنْكَ قَوْلُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: تَكْذِيبُهُمْ لَكَ وَكُفْرُهُمْ بِاللَّهِ، ﴿إِنَّا نَعْلَمُ مَا يُسِرُّونَ وَمَا يُعْلِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: نَحْنُ نَعْلَمُ جَمِيعَ مَا هُمْ عَلَيْهِ، وَسَنَجْزِيهِمْ وصْفَهم وَنُعَامِلُهُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، يَوْمَ لَا يَفْقِدُونَ مِنْ أَعْمَالِهِمْ جَلِيلًا وَلَا حَقِيرًا، وَلَا صَغِيرًا وَلَا كَبِيرًا، بَلْ يُعْرَضُ عَلَيْهِمْ جَمِيعُ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ قَدِيمًا وَحَدِيثًا.

---

## 36:77-80 — verses 77-80 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Mujahid, Ikrimah, Urwah ibn al-Zubayr, al-Suddi, and Qatadah said: Ubayy ibn Khalaf (may Allah curse him) came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ with a decayed bone in his hand, crumbling it and scattering it in the air, saying: "O Muhammad, do you claim that Allah will resurrect this?" He said: "Yes. Allah will cause you to die, then will resurrect you, then will gather you into the Fire." And these verses from the end of "Ya Sin" were revealed: {Does not man consider that We created him from a drop of sperm} to the end of them.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ali ibn al-Husayn ibn al-Junayd, [chain] Muhammad ibn al-Ala, [chain] Uthman ibn Sa'id al-Zayyat, from Hushaym, from Abu Bishr, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, that al-Asi ibn Wa'il took a bone from the valley floor and crumbled it with his hand, then said to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ: "Will Allah bring this to life after what I see?" The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Yes. Allah will cause you to die, then bring you to life, then admit you into Hell." He said: and the verses at the end of "Ya Sin" were revealed.

Ibn Jarir related it from Ya'qub ibn Ibrahim, from Hushaym, from Abu Bishr, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and mentioned it, but did not mention "Ibn Abbas."

It was also related through the route of al-Awfi, from Ibn Abbas, who said: Abdullah ibn Ubayy came with a bone and crumbled it, and he mentioned something similar to what preceded.

This is munkar (a rejected report), because the surah is Meccan, while Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul was only present in Medina. In any case, whether these verses were revealed concerning Ubayy ibn Khalaf, or concerning al-Asi ibn Wa'il, or concerning both of them, they are general, applying to everyone who denies the resurrection. The alif and lam in His saying {Does not man consider} indicate the genus (indicating the general class), encompassing every denier of the resurrection.

{that We created him from a drop of sperm, and then he is a manifest disputant}, meaning: does he who denies the resurrection not draw an inference from the beginning of creation regarding its repetition? For Allah began the creation of man from an extract of despicable fluid, creating him from something insignificant, weak, and lowly, as He, the Exalted, said: {Did We not create you from a despicable fluid, then We placed it in a secure resting place, until a known term?} [al-Mursalat: 20-22]. And He said: {Indeed, We created man from a drop of sperm, a mixture, testing him} [al-Insan: 2], meaning: from a drop composed of scattered mixed elements. So the One who created him from this weak drop, is He not able to bring him back after his death? As Imam Ahmad said in his Musnad:

[chain] Abu al-Mughirah, [chain] Hariz, [chain] Abd al-Rahman ibn Maysarah, from Jubayr ibn Nufayr, from Busr ibn Jahhash, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ spat one day into his palm, placed his finger upon it, then said: "Allah, the Exalted, said: O son of Adam, how can you defy Me when I created you from something like this? Then when I had shaped you and made you upright, you walked between your two garments, and the earth had a heavy tread from you. You gathered and you withheld, until when death reached your collarbones, you said: 'Shall I give charity?' But when is the time for charity?"

Ibn Majah related it from Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah, from Yazid ibn Harun, from Jarir ibn Uthman, with the same wording. For this reason He said: {And he presents for Us an example, forgetting his own creation. He says: Who will give life to the bones when they are decayed?} That is: he considered it far-fetched that Allah, possessor of the tremendous power that created the heavens and the earth, could restore bodies and decayed bones, forgetting himself, and that Allah created him from nothing. He was aware, from his own self, of something more astonishing than what he deemed impossible, denied, and rejected. For this reason, Allah, the Exalted, said: {Say: He who produced them the first time will give them life. And He is All-Knowing of every creation}, meaning: He knows where the bones are in all the regions and corners of the earth, where they have gone, and where they have been scattered and torn apart.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Affan, [chain] Abu Awanah, from Abd al-Malik ibn Umayr, from Rib'i, who said: Uqbah ibn Amr said to Hudhayfah: "Will you not tell us what you heard from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ?" He said: I heard him say: "A man was approached by death, and when he despaired of life, he instructed his family: 'When I die, gather for me abundant thick firewood, then light a fire in it, until it has consumed my flesh and reached my bones, and they are charred. Then take them, crush them, and scatter them into the sea.' They did so. Then Allah gathered him to Himself and said to him: 'Why did you do that?' He said: 'Out of fear of You.' So Allah forgave him." Uqbah ibn Amr said: I too heard him say that, and he was a grave-robber.

Both [Bukhari and Muslim] related it in the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Abd al-Malik ibn Umayr, with many wordings, among them: that he commanded his sons to burn him, then grind him fine, then scatter half of him on land and half of him in the sea, on a windy day, that is, a day of much wind. They did so. Then Allah commanded the sea, and it gathered what was in it, and He commanded the land, and it gathered what was in it. Then He said to him: "Be." And there he was, a man standing. He said to him: "What made you do what you did?" He said: "Fear of You, and You know best." So Allah did nothing to him except that He forgave him.

And His saying: {He who made for you fire from the green tree, and then you kindle from it}, meaning: He who began the creation of this tree from water until it became green and flourishing, bearing fruit and ripeness, then returned it until it became dry firewood by which fire is kindled. Thus He does whatever He wills, and is capable of whatever He desires; nothing prevents Him.

Qatadah said regarding His saying {He who made for you fire from the green tree, and then you kindle from it}: he means, He who brought forth this fire from this tree is able to resurrect him.

It has also been said that what is meant by this is the marakh and afar shrubs, which grow in the land of the Hijaz. One who wishes to strike a fire but has no flint takes two green branches from it and strikes one against the other, and fire is generated between them, just like flint striking. This was related from Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with both of them. And in the proverb: "Every tree has fire, but the marakh and afar have excelled in it." The wise men said: "In every tree there is fire, except the reed."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وعِكْرِمَة، وَعُرْوَةُ بْنُ الزُّبَيْرِ، والسُّدِّي. وَقَتَادَةُ: جَاءَ أُبي بْنُ خَلَفٍ [لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ] إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَفِي يَدِهِ عَظْمٌ رَمِيمٌ وَهُوَ يُفَتِّتُه وَيُذْرِيهِ فِي الْهَوَاءِ، وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، أَتَزْعُمُ أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَبْعَثُ هَذَا؟ فَقَالَ: "نَعَمْ، يُمِيتُكَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى ثُمَّ يَبْعَثُكَ، ثُمَّ يَحْشُرُكَ إِلَى النَّارِ". وَنَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَاتُ مِنْ آخِرِ "يس": ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَ الإنْسَانُ أَنَّا خَلَقْنَاهُ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ﴾ ، إِلَى آخِرِهِنَّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الحسين بْنِ الْجُنَيْدِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْعَلَاءِ، حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ سَعِيدٍ الزَّيَّاتُ، عَنْ هُشَيْم، عَنْ أَبِي بِشْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ ، عَنِ ابن عباس، أن العاصى بْنَ وَائِلٍ أَخَذَ عَظْمًا مِنَ الْبَطْحَاءِ ففتَّه بِيَدِهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: أَيُحْيِي اللَّهُ هَذَا بَعْدَ مَا أَرَى؟ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "نَعَمْ، يُمِيتُكَ اللَّهُ ثُمَّ يُحْيِيكَ، ثُمَّ يدخلك جهنم". قال: وَنَزَلَتِ الْآيَاتُ مِنْ آخَرِ "يس".

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ يَعْقُوبَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ هُشَيْمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي بِشْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، فَذَكَرَهُ وَلَمْ يَذْكُرِ "ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ" .

وَرُوِيَ مِنْ طَرِيقِ الْعَوْفِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أُبَيٍّ بِعَظْمٍ ففَتَّه وَذَكَرَ نَحْوَ مَا تَقَدَّمَ.

وَهَذَا مُنْكَرٌ؛ لِأَنَّ السُّورَةَ مكية، وعبد الله بن أبي بن سَلُولَ إِنَّمَا كَانَ بِالْمَدِينَةِ. وَعَلَى كُلِّ تَقْدِيرٍ سَوَاءً كَانَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَاتُ قَدْ نَزَلَتْ فِي أُبي بْنِ خَلَفٍ، أَوْ [فِي] الْعَاصِ [بْنِ وَائِلٍ] ، أَوْ فِيهِمَا، فَهِيَ عَامَّةٌ فِي كُلِّ مَنْ أَنْكَرَ الْبَعْثَ. وَالْأَلِفُ وَاللَّامُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَ الإنْسَانُ﴾ لِلْجِنْسِ، يَعُمُّ كُلَّ مُنْكِرٍ لِلْبَعْثِ.

﴿أَنَّا خَلَقْنَاهُ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ فَإِذَا هُوَ خَصِيمٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: أَوْلَمَ يَسْتَدِلَّ مَنْ أَنْكَرَ الْبَعْثَ بِالْبَدْءِ عَلَى الْإِعَادَةِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ ابْتَدَأَ خَلْقَ الْإِنْسَانِ مِنْ سُلَالَةٍ مِنْ مَاءٍ مَهِينٍ، فَخَلَقَهُ مِنْ شَيْءٍ حَقِيرٍ ضَعِيفٍ مَهِينٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلَمْ نَخْلُقْكُمْ مِنْ مَاءٍ مَهِينٍ * فَجَعَلْنَاهُ فِي قَرَارٍ مَكِينٍ * إِلَى قَدَرٍ مَعْلُومٍ﴾ [الْمُرْسَلَاتِ: ٢٠-٢٢] . وَقَالَ ﴿إِنَّا خَلَقْنَا الإنْسَانَ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ أَمْشَاجٍ نَبْتَلِيهِ﴾ [الْإِنْسَانِ: ٢] أَيْ: مَنْ نُطْفَةٍ مِنْ أَخْلَاطٍ مُتَفَرِّقَةٍ، فَالَّذِي خَلَقَهُ مِنْ هَذِهِ النُّطْفَةِ الضَّعِيفَةِ أَلَيْسَ بِقَادِرٍ عَلَى إِعَادَتِهِ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهِ؟ كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْمُغِيرَةِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَريز، حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَيْسَرة، عَنْ جُبَيْر بْنِ نُفَيْرٍ، عَنْ بُسْر ابن جَحَّاش؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَصق يَوْمًا فِي كفِّه، فَوَضَعَ عَلَيْهَا أُصْبُعَهُ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ابْنَ آدَمَ، أنَّى تُعجزني وَقَدْ خَلَقْتُكَ مِنْ مِثْلِ هَذِهِ، حَتَّى إِذَا سَوَّيتك وعَدَلتك، مَشَيْتَ بَيْنَ بردَيك وَلِلْأَرْضِ مِنْكَ وَئِيدٌ، فَجَمَعْتَ وَمَنَعْتَ، حَتَّى إِذَا بَلَغَت التَّرَاقِي قُلْتَ: أتصدقُ وأنَّى أَوَانُ الصَّدَقَةِ؟ ".

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ هَارُونَ، عَنْ جَرير بْنِ عُثْمَانَ، بِهِ . وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَضَرَبَ لَنَا مَثَلا وَنَسِيَ خَلْقَهُ قَالَ مَنْ يُحْيِي الْعِظَامَ وَهِيَ رَمِيمٌ﴾ ؟ أَيِ: اسْتَبْعَدَ إِعَادَةَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى -ذِي الْقُدْرَةِ الْعَظِيمَةِ الَّتِي خَلَقَتِ السموات وَالْأَرْضَ-لِلْأَجْسَادِ وَالْعِظَامِ الرَّمِيمَةِ، وَنَسِيَ نَفْسَهُ، وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَهُ مِنَ الْعَدَمِ، فَعَلِمَ مِنْ نَفْسِهِ مَا هُوَ أَعْظَمُ مِمَّا اسْتَبْعَدَهُ وَأَنْكَرَهُ وَجَحَدَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ يُحْيِيهَا الَّذِي أَنْشَأَهَا أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ خَلْقٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْلَمُ الْعِظَامَ فِي سَائِرِ أَقْطَارِ الْأَرْضِ وَأَرْجَائِهَا، أَيْنَ ذَهَبَتْ، وَأَيْنَ تَفَرَّقَتْ وَتَمَزَّقَتْ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَوَانة، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ، عَنْ رِبْعيّ قَالَ: قَالَ عُقْبَةُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو لِحُذَيْفَةَ: أَلَا تحدثُنا مَا سمعتَ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟ فَقَالَ: سَمِعْتُهُ يَقُولُ: "إِنْ رَجُلًا حَضَرَهُ الْمَوْتُ، فَلَمَّا أَيِسَ مِنَ الْحَيَاةِ أَوْصَى أَهْلَهُ: إِذَا أَنَا مُتُّ فَاجْمَعُوا لِي حَطَبا كثيرًا جزَلا ثُمَّ أَوْقَدُوا فِيهِ نَارًا، حَتَّى إِذَا [أَكَلَتْ] لَحْمِي وخلَصت إِلَى عَظْمِي فامتُحِشْتُ، فَخُذُوهَا فَدُقُّوهَا فَذَروها فِي الْيَمِّ. فَفَعَلُوا، فَجَمَعَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ فَقَالَ لَهُ: لِمَ فَعَلْتَ ذَلِكَ؟ قَالَ: مِنْ خَشْيَتِكَ. فَغَفَرَ اللَّهُ لَهُ". فَقَالَ عُقْبَةُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو: وَأَنَا سُمْعَتُهُ يَقُولُ ذَلِكَ، وَكَانَ نبَّاشا. 

وَقَدْ أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ، بِأَلْفَاظٍ كَثِيرَةٍ مِنْهَا: أَنَّهُ أَمَرَ بَنِيهِ أَنْ يَحْرُقُوهُ ثُمَّ يَسْحَقُوهُ، ثُمَّ يَذْروا نِصْفَهُ فِي الْبَرِّ وَنِصْفَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ، فِي يَوْمٍ رَائِحٍ، أَيْ: كَثِيرِ الْهَوَاءِ -فَفَعَلُوا ذَلِكَ. فَأَمَرَ اللَّهُ الْبَحْرَ فَجَمَعَ مَا فِيهِ، وَأَمَرَ الْبَرَّ فَجَمَعَ مَا فِيهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ لَهُ: كُنْ. فَإِذَا هُوَ رَجُلٌ قَائِمٌ. فَقَالَ لَهُ: مَا حَمَلَكَ عَلَى مَا صَنَعْتَ؟ فَقَالَ: مَخَافَتُكَ وَأَنْتَ أَعْلَمُ. فَمَا تَلَافَاهُ أَنْ غَفَرَ لَهُ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿الَّذِي جَعَلَ لَكُمْ مِنَ الشَّجَرِ الأخْضَرِ نَارًا فَإِذَا أَنْتُمْ مِنْهُ تُوقِدُونَ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي بَدَأَ خَلْقَ هَذَا الشَّجَرِ مِنْ مَاءٍ حَتَّى صَارَ خَضرًا نَضرًا ذَا ثَمَرٍ ويَنْع، ثُمَّ أَعَادَهُ إِلَى أَنْ صَارَ حَطَبًا يَابِسًا، تُوقَدُ بِهِ النَّارُ، كَذَلِكَ هُوَ فَعَّالٌ لِمَا يَشَاءُ، قَادِرٌ عَلَى مَا يُرِيدُ لَا يَمْنَعُهُ شَيْءٌ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿الَّذِي جَعَلَ لَكُمْ مِنَ الشَّجَرِ الأخْضَرِ نَارًا فَإِذَا أَنْتُمْ مِنْهُ تُوقِدُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ: الَّذِي أَخْرَجَ هَذِهِ النَّارَ مِنْ هَذَا الشَّجَرِ قَادِرٌ عَلَى أَنْ يَبْعَثَهُ.

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِذَلِكَ سَرْح الْمَرْخِ والعَفَار، يَنْبُتُ فِي أَرْضِ الْحِجَازِ فَيَأْتِي مَنْ أَرَادَ قَدْح نَارٍ وَلَيْسَ مَعَهُ زِنَادٌ، فَيَأْخُذُ مِنْهُ عُودَيْنِ أَخْضَرَيْنِ، وَيَقْدَحُ أَحَدَهُمَا بِالْآخَرِ، فَتَتَوَلَّدُ النَّارُ مِنْ بَيْنِهِمَا، كَالزِّنَادِ سَوَاءً. رُوِيَ هَذَا عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا . وَفِي الْمَثَلِ: لِكُلِّ شَجَرٍ نَارٌ، وَاسْتَمْجَدَ المَرْخُ والعَفَار. وَقَالَ الْحُكَمَاءُ: فِي كُلِّ شَجَرٍ نَارٌ إِلَّا الْغَابَ.

---

## 36:81-83 — verses 81-83 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, drawing attention to His tremendous power in creating the seven heavens with what they contain of moving and fixed stars, and the seven earths with what they contain of mountains and sands, seas and deserts, and what lies between all that, and guiding to the proof of the return of bodies through the creation of these great things, as in His saying: {The creation of the heavens and the earth is greater than the creation of mankind} [Ghafir: 57]. And He says here: {Is not the One who created the heavens and the earth able to create the like of them}, meaning the like of mankind, so that He may bring them back as He originated them. So said Ibn Jarir.

This verse is like His saying: {Do they not see that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth and did not tire in creating them, is able to give life to the dead? Yes indeed, He is over all things capable} [al-Ahqaf: 33], and like His saying: {Yes indeed, and He is the All-Knowing Creator. His command, when He wills a thing, is only to say to it "Be," and it is}, meaning He commands the thing with a single command, needing no repetition:

When Allah wills a matter, He only says to it "Be," a single utterance, and it is.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... from Abu Dharr, may Allah be pleased with him, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah says: O My servants, all of you are sinners except the one I have spared, so seek My forgiveness and I will forgive you. And all of you are poor except the one I have made wealthy. I am generous, glorious, ever-abounding, I do what I will. My giving is a word, and My punishment is a word. When I will a thing, I only say to it 'Be,' and it is."

His saying: {So glorified is the One in whose hand is the dominion (malakut) of all things, and to Him you will be returned} means: exaltation, sanctification, and clearing from any evil, of the Ever-Living, the Self-Subsisting, in whose hand are the keys of the heavens and the earth, and to whom all matters return, to whom belong creation and command, and to whom the servants will be returned on the Day of Resurrection, so that He may reward every worker for his work. He is the Just, the Bestower of favor.

The meaning of His saying: {So glorified is the One in whose hand is the malakut of all things} is like His saying, Mighty and Exalted is He: {Say: In whose hand is the malakut of all things} [al-Mu'minun: 88], and like His saying: {Blessed is the One in whose hand is the dominion (al-mulk)} [al-Mulk: 1]. So al-mulk and al-malakut are one in meaning, like rahmah (mercy) and rahamut, rahbah (fear) and rahabut, jabr (compulsion) and jabarut. Some people have claimed that al-mulk is the world of bodies while al-malakut is the world of spirits, but the first view is the correct one, and it is what the majority of the commentators and others hold.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... from Hudhayfah, that is Ibn al-Yaman, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: I stood in prayer with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ one night, and he recited the seven long surahs in seven cycles (rak'ahs). When he raised his head from bowing (ruku') he would say: "Allah hears the one who praises Him." Then he would say: "Praise belongs to the Possessor of malakut, jabarut, greatness, and majesty." His bowing was like his standing, and his prostration was like his bowing. So I departed and my legs were nearly about to break.

Abu Dawud, al-Tirmidhi in al-Shama'il, and al-Nasa'i related, from the hadith of Shu'bah, from Amr ibn Murrah, from Abu Hamzah, freedman of the Ansar, from a man of Banu Abs, from Hudhayfah: that he saw the Messenger of Allah ﷺ at night, and he used to say: "Allah is the Greatest," three times, "the Possessor of malakut, jabarut, greatness, and majesty." Then he opened with the recitation and read Surat al-Baqarah, then he bowed, and his bowing was about equal to his standing, and he used to say in his bowing: "Glory be to my Lord the Tremendous." Then he raised his head from bowing, and his standing was about equal to his bowing, saying: "To my Lord belongs praise." Then he prostrated, and his prostration was about equal to his standing, and he used to say in his prostration: "Glory be to my Lord the Most High." Then he raised his head from prostration, and he used to sit between the two prostrations for about as long as his prostration, saying: "My Lord, forgive me, my Lord, forgive me." He prayed four cycles (rak'ahs), reciting in them al-Baqarah, Al Imran, al-Nisa, and al-Ma'idah, or al-An'am, Shu'bah being uncertain. This is the wording of Abu Dawud.

Al-Nasa'i said: "Abu Hamzah according to us is Talhah ibn Yazid, and this man appears likely to be Silah." So he said. But it seems more likely that he was the cousin of Hudhayfah, as was mentioned earlier in the report of Imam Ahmad, and Allah knows best. As for the report of Silah ibn Zufar from Hudhayfah, it is found in Sahih Muslim, but it does not mention malakut, jabarut, greatness, and majesty.

Abu Dawud said: [chain] ... from Awf ibn Malik al-Ashja'i, who said: I stood in prayer with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ one night, and he stood and recited Surat al-Baqarah. He would not pass by a verse of mercy without stopping and asking for it, nor pass by a verse of punishment without stopping and seeking refuge from it. He said: Then he bowed for a duration equal to his standing, saying in his bowing: "Glory be to the Possessor of jabarut, malakut, greatness, and majesty." Then he prostrated for a duration equal to his standing, then said the same in his prostration. Then he stood and recited Al Imran, then he recited surah after surah.

Al-Tirmidhi related it in al-Shama'il, and al-Nasa'i, from the hadith of Mu'awiyah ibn Salih, with this wording.

The end of the commentary on Surat Ya-Sin. To Allah belongs all praise, first and last, outwardly and inwardly.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُنَبِّهًا عَلَى قُدْرَتِهِ الْعَظِيمَةِ فِي خلق السموات السَّبْعِ، بِمَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْكَوَاكِبِ السَّيَّارَةِ وَالثَّوَابِتِ، وَالْأَرْضِينَ السَّبْعِ وَمَا فِيهَا مِنْ جِبَالٍ وَرِمَالٍ، وَبِحَارٍ وَقَفَارٍ، وَمَا بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ، وَمُرْشِدًا إِلَى الِاسْتِدْلَالِ عَلَى إِعَادَةِ الْأَجْسَادِ بِخَلْقِ هَذِهِ الْأَشْيَاءِ العظيمة، كقوله تعالى: ﴿لَخَلْقُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ أَكْبَرُ مِنْ خَلْقِ النَّاسِ﴾ [غَافِرٍ: ٥٧] . وَقَالَ هاهنا: ﴿أَوَلَيْسَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ بِقَادِرٍ عَلَى أَنْ يَخْلُقَ مِثْلَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِثْلَ الْبَشَرِ، فَيُعِيدُهُمْ كَمَا بَدَأَهُمْ. قَالَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ. 

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّ اللَّهَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ وَلَمْ يَعْيَ بِخَلْقِهِنَّ بِقَادِرٍ عَلَى أَنْ يُحْيِيَ الْمَوْتَى بَلَى إِنَّهُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ [الأحقاف: ٣٣] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿بَلَى وَهُوَ الْخَلاقُ الْعَلِيمُ إِنَّمَا أَمْرُهُ إِذَا أَرَادَ شَيْئًا أَنْ يَقُولَ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ﴾ أَيْ: يَأْمُرُ بِالشَّيْءِ أَمْرًا وَاحِدًا، لَا يَحْتَاجُ إِلَى تَكْرَارٍ:

إذَا مَا أَرَادَ اللهُ أَمْرًا فَإِنَّمَا ... يَقُولُ لَهُ "كُنْ" قَوْلَة فَيَكُونُ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ نُمَيْر، حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ المسَيَّب، عَنْ شَهْر، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ غَنْم، عَنْ أَبِي ذَر، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: يَا عِبَادِي، كُلُّكُمْ مُذْنِبٌ إِلَّا مِنْ عَافَيْتُ، فَاسْتَغْفِرُونِي أَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ. وَكُلُّكُمْ فَقِيرٌ إِلَّا مَنْ أَغْنَيْتُ، إِنِّي جَوَادٌ مَاجِدٌ وَاجِدٌ أَفْعَلُ مَا أَشَاءُ، عَطَائِي كَلَامٌ، وَعَذَابِي كَلَامٌ، إِذَا أَرَدْتُ شَيْئًا فَإِنَّمَا أَقُولُ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ". 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَسُبْحَانَ الَّذِي بِيَدِهِ مَلَكُوتُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَإِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: تَنْزِيهٌ وَتَقْدِيسٌ وَتَبْرِئَةٌ مِنَ السُّوءِ لِلْحَيِّ القيوم، الذي بيده مقاليد السموات وَالْأَرْضِ، وَإِلَيْهِ يَرْجِعُ الْأَمْرُ كُلُّهُ، وَلَهُ الْخَلْقُ وَالْأَمْرُ، وَإِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُ الْعِبَادُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَيُجَازِي كُلَّ عَامِلٍ بِعَمَلِهِ، وَهُوَ الْعَادِلُ الْمُتَفَضِّلُ.

وَمَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَسُبْحَانَ الَّذِي بِيَدِهِ مَلَكُوتُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿قُلْ مَنْ بِيَدِهِ مَلَكُوتُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ٨٨] ، وَكَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿تَبَارَكَ الَّذِي بِيَدِهِ الْمُلْكُ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ: ١] ، فَالْمُلْكُ وَالْمَلَكُوتُ وَاحِدٌ فِي الْمَعْنَى، كَرَحْمَةٍ ورَحَمُوت، ورَهْبَة ورَهَبُوت، وجَبْر وجَبَرُوت. وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ زَعَمَ أَنَّ المُلْك هُوَ عَالَمُ الْأَجْسَادِ وَالْمَلَكُوتَ هُوَ عَالَمُ الْأَرْوَاحِ، وَالْأَوَّلُ هُوَ الصَّحِيحُ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي عَلَيْهِ الْجُمْهُورُ مِنَ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ وَغَيْرِهِمْ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادٌ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ، حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ عَمٍّ لِحُذَيْفَةَ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ -وَهُوَ ابْنُ الْيَمَانِ-رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قُمْتُ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ ذَاتَ لَيْلَةٍ، فَقَرَأَ السَّبْعَ الطُّوَل فِي سَبْعِ رَكَعَاتٍ، وَكَانَ إِذَا رَفَعَ رَأْسَهُ مِنَ الرُّكُوعِ قَالَ: "سَمِعَ اللَّهُ لِمَنْ حَمِدَهُ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "الْحَمْدُ لِذِي ذِي الْمَلَكُوتِ وَالْجَبَرُوتِ وَالْكِبْرِيَاءِ وَالْعَظَمَةِ" وَكَانَ رُكُوعُهُ مِثْلَ قِيَامِهِ، وَسُجُودُهُ مِثْلَ رُكُوعِهِ، فَأَنْصَرِفُ وَقَدْ كَادَتْ تَنْكَسِرُ رِجْلَايَ. 

وَقَدْ رَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي الشَّمَائِلِ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرة، عَنْ أَبِي حَمْزة -مَوْلَى الْأَنْصَارِ-عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنْ بَنِي عَبْس، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ؛ أَنَّهُ رَأَى رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ، وَكَانَ يَقُولُ: "اللَّهُ أَكْبَرُ -ثَلَاثًا -ذُو الْمَلَكُوتِ وَالْجَبَرُوتِ وَالْكِبْرِيَاءِ وَالْعَظَمَةِ". ثُمَّ اسْتَفْتَحَ فَقَرَأَ الْبَقَرَةَ، ثُمَّ رَكَعَ فَكَانَ رُكُوعُهُ نَحْوًا مِنْ قِيَامِهِ، وَكَانَ يَقُولُ فِي رُكُوعِهِ: "سُبْحَانَ رَبِّيَ الْعَظِيمِ". ثُمَّ رَفَعَ رَأْسَهُ مِنَ الرُّكُوعِ، فَكَانَ قِيَامُهُ نَحْوًا مِنْ] رُكُوعِهِ، يَقُولُ: " لِرَبِّي الْحَمْدُ". ثُمَّ سَجَدَ، فَكَانَ سُجُودُهُ نَحْوًا مِنْ] قِيَامِهِ، وَكَانَ يَقُولُ فِي سجوده: "سبحان ربي الأعلى". ثم رفع رَأْسَهُ مِنَ السُّجُودِ، وَكَانَ يَقْعُدُ فِيمَا بَيْنُ السَّجْدَتَيْنِ نَحْوًا مِنْ سُجُودِهِ، وَكَانَ يَقُولُ: "رَبِّ، اغْفِرْ لِي، رَبِّ اغْفِرْ لِي". فَصَلَّى أَرْبَعَ رَكَعَاتٍ، فَقَرَأَ فِيهِنَّ الْبَقَرَةَ، وَآلَ عِمْرَانَ، وَالنِّسَاءَ، وَالْمَائِدَةَ -أَوِ الْأَنْعَامَ --شَكَّ شُعْبَةُ-هَذَا لَفْظُ أَبِي دَاوُدَ. 

وَقَالَ النَّسَائِيُّ: "أَبُو حَمْزَةَ عِنْدَنَا: طَلْحَةُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ، وَهَذَا الرَّجُلُ يُشْبِهُ أَنْ يَكُونَ صِلَةً". كَذَا قَالَ. وَالْأَشْبَهُ أَنْ يَكُونَ ابْنَ عَمِّ حُذَيْفَةَ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ فِي رِوَايَةِ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ، [وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ] . فَأَمَّا رِوَايَةُ صِلَةَ بْنِ زُفَرَ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ، فَإِنَّهَا فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، وَلَكِنْ لَيْسَ فِيهَا ذِكْرُ الْمَلَكُوتِ وَالْجَبَرُوتِ وَالْكِبْرِيَاءِ وَالْعَظَمَةِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ صَالِحٍ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، حَدَّثَنِي مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ صَالِحٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ قَيْسٍ، عَنْ عَاصِمِ بْنِ حُمَيْد، عَنْ عَوْفِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ الْأَشْجَعِيِّ قَالَ: قمتُ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَيْلَةً فَقَامَ فَقَرَأَ سُورَةَ الْبَقَرَةِ، لَا يَمُرُّ بِآيَةِ رَحْمَةٍ إِلَّا وَقَفَ فَسَأَلَ، وَلَا يَمُرُّ بِآيَةِ عَذَابٍ إِلَّا وَقَفَ فَتَعَوَّذَ. قَالَ: ثُمَّ رَكَعَ بِقَدْرِ قِيَامِهِ، يَقُولُ فِي رُكُوعِهِ: "سُبْحَانَ ذِي الْجَبَرُوتِ وَالْمَلَكُوتِ وَالْكِبْرِيَاءِ وَالْعَظَمَةِ". ثُمَّ سَجَدَ بِقَدْرِ قِيَامِهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ فِي سُجُودِهِ مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ قَامَ فَقَرَأَ بِآلِ عِمْرَانَ، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ سُورَةً سُورَةً.

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي الشَّمَائِلِ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، بِهِ. 

] آخِرُ تَفْسِيرِ سُورَةِ "يس" ولله الحمد أولا وآخرًا وظاهرًا وباطنًا]

---
